Dr. Lopez is beyond words. My daughter is in LOVE with him. She asks if she can just go say Hi to him or take him a snack...lol He's made my daughters asthma almost nonexistent. For that she is extremely grateful. Most times there is a loooong wait but, he is the BEST and comes highly recommend(by my daughter) and many others.

His nursing assistant on the other hand makes it extremely cumbersome to leave him a message per his request knowing its in regards to asthma and time is of the essence. Sensitivity training is definitely needed. Over all EVERYONE else is very nice and helpful. I am grateful for this facility.
Thank you Eisner Health Dr.'s and staff.<//Review>

< Text>
Solid 5 stars, had to take one star of for insects see rest for details.
I underestimated the amount of mosquitoes in dry September and gotten eaten alive. Good idea to have hat and bug net on sections to avoid eating/inhaling or get eaten by flies.
Other then that spectacular canyon, nice trails, beautiful river, clean nice crowd. Narrows as you move past mist falls. The trees have are suffering fires, drought, invasive beetles? BTW is no coverage.< /Text>

In fact, Toyota does not even recommend Nitrogen to be used, in place of regular air.  Although Nitrogen does have some benefits, its benefits are not substantial enough to justify its cost.  It's a product that benefits the seller a lot more than it benefits the buyer, or the customer, so we have made the decision to not sell it.  Believe it or not, every decision we make at Mojave Auto Group is with our customers' well being and benefit in mind.  If and when Toyota decides that Nitrogen filled tires are actually cost effective and a benefit to the customers, you will see every Toyota vehicle come from the factory with Nitrogen filled tires, and you will see every Toyota dealer, including us, offer Nitrogen Gas in our Service Departments.\nSo if you're upset with us for not carrying the Nitrogen Gas, a product that's not offered or even recommended by Toyota, maybe you're being a bit harsh in your judgment.  We do whatever it takes to earn our customers' business, and every now and then, we fail, but when we do fail, we always accept the blame, apologize, and try to make it up to our customers.  I hope we get the opportunity to prove to you that you should keep your business in town.\nI am at a loss for words when it comes to one of our salespeople showing you a Corolla, when you were interested in a Highlander.  I hope that salesperson is no longer with us.  We don't decide what a customer purchases, nor does it make a difference to us what we sell.  The only time we suggest a different vehicle is when and if the banks limit us to the amount they would lend a customer.  I don't think that was the case with you, since it doesn't seem like you were at our store long enough for us to go that far into the deal.  I have no idea why a salesperson would show you a Corolla, when you were interested in a Highlander, since the two units aren't at all alike. In this case, you benefited, and saved yourself a lot of money, that is a good thing.  That, certainly, shouldn't cause you to have a negative opinion of us.  I could understand if you had gotten the lower price from a different dealership, but we're the same store that saved you all of that money.\nIn any event, I am not at the store today, so I am not sure if you've already picked up your Jeep, but I can assure you that if the Internet price was that much less than what our salesperson had given you as his rock bottom price, you're buying the Jeep below what we paid for it, which makes it a great deal for you.  Yes, we do sometimes sell our vehicles below what we paid for them, in order to earn our customers' business, and to add to our family and customer base.\nNot only that, you'll also receive a $500 Gift Card from us that you can use for your future automotive needs. <pictures>None</pictures>< text>
I'm skeptical about going to any urgent care, I'd just rather go to ER than an urgent care.
However, back in December I decided to try Modern Urgent Care.

I was in and out in a short amount of time. Their service is the best!  Clean,  fast, friendly, professional, and their doctors are the exceptional.

I'm going to make an appointment with one of their doctors, Dr Robert Ginther (From Ceres),  who treated me at Modern Urgent Care back in December.   His practice is in Ceres, but I was so pleased with his service, confidence,  and professionalism that I don't mind going out of town to see a primary who cares, and gives good service.

Yesterday, March 7th, was my second time there. I was there for two different issues yesterday, and had to have surgery on my toe for an ingrown toenail.  My main worry was how my toe and toenail would look after the surgery. The doctor who helped me was a student, Jacob. But if you saw the incision, you would think his hands have built in lasers because you can't even tell I had surgery. It's such a clean cut. I am so pleased and still can't believe how well the results of this surgery are.

Im  still skeptical about going to  urgent care, but not  Modern Urgent Care. I will tell my family and friends about my experiences there, and continue to go there if necessary. Thank you Modern Urgent Care for the great all around service you proceeded me with.< /text>
